Site For Sore Eyes is absolutely Outstanding!  Yes, they have really cool styles (I found at least 6 pair I Loved - which doesn't ever happen) and every name brand that would make a eyeglass aficionado feel like they won the lottery. <Review>Came here after a 2.5 hour hike, so we were famished. Got seated immediately as it wasn't crowded at all for a Sunday afternoon. We ordered the croissant, iced latte, white mocha and the egg florentine and spinach and goat cheese quiche with french fries.

The croissant was soft and tasty. My boyfriend thought it was not flaky enough, but I love the soft, non-flaky croissants that don't fall apart after a bite, so I was happy.

The iced latte was a bit too iced and not very interesting. However, the white mocha was very well made - enough sweetness for someone like me who puts 3 sugars in her coffee and also enough bitterness for my boyfriend who puts no sugar in his.

The florentine was tasty enough. I particularly do not enjoy the runny yolk, but the bread was well made and the whole thing worked. The potatoes were lovely. The fruits on the side made for a refreshing meal.

The quiche was ok. I could not taste the goat cheese until the very last bite. I guess it was like every other spinach and goat cheese quiche. The salad accompanying was delicious! (I am not a salad person at all). Since I'd asked for french fries and they served the salad by mistake, they also served the french fries, which were also delicious - thin, hot and not very salty.

All in all, the meal was very filling, the owner was very nice. However, not sure that the food was extra-ordinary.< /Review>< pics>

< text>
Customers: Please wear a mask to get take out. Transmission of COVID-19 to those who run China Wok would be a disaster for this family and a loss for this community.

I have been going to China Wok for over 24 years. It's like the corner pub, but for Chinese food. Very friendly with many regular customers. I get my lunch (takeout) at China Wok almost every day. I get the 2-item combo for $7.94 including tax. Their food is the best, the portions are large, and you can't beat the price. Service is terrific. They know each customer, what they usually get, and aim to please. I love their mushroom chicken, which also has zucchini and carrots, but I've had many different items and they are all good. I don't eat deep fried items (too many empty calories), so I can't comment on Orange Chicken, etc., but items that are not deep fried are not greasy at all and not as salty as other places with more expensive food. Wonderful flavor. I look forward to it every day.

You should be aware that they don't take credit/debit cards. That keeps their costs low, so it's for the best, in my opinion. It's the only place I use cash, and well worth it!< /text>

< Text>
Very friendly service, a wide selection of raspados, juices, snacks, and the best part is if you want to personalize your raspado (you can combine flavors) they will make it just they way you like it, just ask. Clean and very attentive. Everyone who works here is happy and friendly. Service with a smile. The fruit is always fresh (they chop everything). Their new paletas have me excited, there are so many flavors, so creamy, so delicious. The cheese paleta is one of my favorite. They have something for everyone.< /Text>

< Review>
Woah, so many juice options! Their root beer floats aren't bad either. I went here on a typical LA hot AF summer day and was super parched after riding my motorcycle. Raspados Zone was in the area and I was fiending something to quench my thirst. Ordered a smoothie and a root beer float because why not. Oh man, the smoothie was made fresh and on the spot, the flavors are all upfront and you can taste how fresh they were, and the root beer float was pretty good too. Just a warning, though; don't do what I did by ordering both a smoothie and a float because you won't be able to finish both.</Review>
